# Welcome! | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/welcome.md)
.

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/#welcome-to-the-onetap-reloaded-lua-api-docs)

Welcome to the **Onetap Reloaded Lua API Docs**!


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Here you’ll find everything you need to get up and running with the Lua API for Onetap Reloaded.

* * *

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/#want-to-jump-right-in)

Want to jump right in?


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Feeling eager? Dive into the quick start docs and start scripting with minimal setup.

[Quick Start](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start)

* * *

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/#want-to-deep-dive)

Want to deep dive?


------------------------------------------------------------------------

Dive a little deeper and start exploring our API reference to get an idea of everything that's possible - all of the libraries/classes have usage examples to help you implement any features you desire.

Last updated 8 months ago

# color | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color.md)
.

Copy

    local clr = color.new(255, 128, 0, 200)
    print("Red component:", clr:r())
    
    -- Default (0, 0, 0, 255)
    local a = color.new()
    
    -- RGB (alpha defaults to 255)
    local b = color.new(255, 128, 0)
    
    -- RGBA
    local c = color.new(255, 128, 0, 200)

Copy

    color.new(integer: r, integer: g, integer: b, [integer: a])

**Parameters**:

*   `r` (`integer`): red component 0-255
    
*   `g` (`integer`): green component 0-255
    
*   `b` (`integer`): blue component 0-255
    
*   `a` (`integer`, optional, default: `255`): alpha (transparency) component 0-255
    

Member

Type

Example Value

`clr:r()`

integer

255

`clr:g()`

integer

128

`clr:b()`

integer

0

`clr:a()`

integer

200

Last updated 10 months ago

# Quick Start | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start.md)
.

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start#callbacks-and-drawing)

Callbacks and drawing:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[register\_callback](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/register_callback)
, [color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
, [rect](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/rect)

A simple showcase of how to use the rendering and color APIs.

Copy

    -- draw callbacks run every frame
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
    
        local clr = color.new(255, 0, 0, 255) -- create a new color
        render.rect(100, 100, 50, 50, clr) -- and use it to render a red rectangle
        -- at x=100, y=100, size: 50x50 px
    
    end)

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start#kill-say)

Kill say


---------------------------------------------------------------------

[register\_callback](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/register_callback)
, [execute\_command](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/execute_command)
, [game\_event](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/game_event)
, [get\_entity\_from\_user\_id](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/entities/get_entity_from_user_id)
, [player](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/player)

Say a message when you kill an enemy or vice versa.

Copy

    local function killsay(event)
        
        local kill = "ez"
        local death = "lucky"
        
        local victim = entities.get_entity_from_user_id(event:get_int("userid"))
        local attacker = entities.get_entity_from_user_id(event:get_int("attacker"))
        
        if not victim then
            return -- check if the victim is a player
        end
        
        if not attacker then
            return -- check if the attacker is a player
        end
        
        if victim:is_local_player() then -- if the local player dies
            cheat.execute_command("say " .. death)
        elseif attacker:is_local_player() then -- if a player is killed by local player
            cheat.execute_command("say " .. kill)
        end
        
    end
    
    -- game event callbacks run when game events occur
    cheat.register_callback("player_death", killsay)

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start#simple-auto-buy)

Simple auto-buy


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[register\_callback](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/register_callback)
, [execute\_command](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/execute_command)
, [game\_event](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/game_event)

A simple automatic buybot that executes on the start of a new round.

Copy

    cheat.register_callback("round_prestart", function()
        
        -- multi-line string
        cheat.execute_command([[buy scar20; buy deagle; buy vest; buy vesthelm;\
        buy incgrenade; buy molotov; buy hegrenade; buy smokegrenade]])
        
    end)

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start#menu-elements)

Menu elements


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[ui](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui)
, [register\_callback](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/register_callback)

A simple checkbox and slider to showcase how the UI API is used.

Copy

    ui.add_checkbox("Check me!")
    ui.add_slider_int("Drag me!", 1, 10)
    
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
        if ui.get_bool("Check me!") then -- check the value of the checkbox
            -- if "Check me!" is checked (and get_bool() returns "true",
            -- print the value of the "Drag me!" slider.
            print("I'm checked and my slider value is "
            .. tostring(ui.get_int("Drag me!")) .. "!")
        end
    end)

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start#advanced-auto-buy)

Advanced auto-buy


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[register\_callback](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/register_callback)
, [ui](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui)
, [execute\_command](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/execute_command)
, [game\_event](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/game_event)

A more advanced automatic buybot that allows you to select which weapons to buy via the UI and runs the command on the start of a new round.

Copy

    local primary = {"", "ak47","ssg08","sg556","awp","scar20","galilar","mac10","mp7","ump45","p90","bizon","nova","xm1014","mag7","m249","negev"}
    local primary_names = {"-", "AK-47 / M4A4 / M4A1-S","SSG 08","SG 553 / AUG","AWP","G3SG1 / SCAR-20","Galil AR / Famas","MAC-10 / MP9","MP7 / MP5-SD","UMP-45","P90","PP-Bizon","Nova","XM1014","Sawed-Off / MAG-7","M249","Negev"}
    
    local secondary = {"", "glock","elite","p250","tec9","deagle"}
    local secondary_names = {"-", "Glock-18 / USP-S / P2000","Dual Berettas","P250","Tec-9 / Five-Seven","Desert Eagle / Revolver"}
    
    local equipment = {"", "vest","vesthelm"}
    local equipment_names = { "-", "Kevlar Vest","Kevlar + Helmet"}
    
    local grenades = {"molotov","decoy","flashbang","flashbang","hegrenade","smokegrenade"}
    local grenades_names = {"Molotov / Incendiary Grenade","Decoy Grenade","Flashbang 1","Flashbang 2","HE Grenade","Smoke Grenade"}
    
    
    -- create all of the UI elements
    ui.add_checkbox("Enable Buybot")
    ui.add_dropdown("Buybot Weapon", primary_names)
    ui.add_dropdown("Buybot Second", secondary_names)
    ui.add_dropdown("Buybot Armor", equipment_names)
    ui.add_checkbox("Buy Zeus x27")
    
    for i, name in pairs(grenades_names) do
        ui.add_checkbox("Buy " .. name)
    end
    
    
    cheat.register_callback("round_prestart", function()
    
        if not ui.get_bool("Enable Buybot") then return end
    
        local buystring = ""
        local val = 0
        
        -- IMPORTANT:
        -- the get_int() function returns the selected item index as a zero-based value.
        -- This means the first element is indexed as 0 (C-style), not 1 (Lua-style)!
        --
        -- In Lua, arrays start at index 1, so you should always add +1 to the value
        -- returned by get_int() when working with dropdowns.
        --
        -- Example:
        -- If get_int() returns 0, it means the first item is selected.
        -- To access the correct element in a Lua table, use:
        --   primary[val + 1]
        --
        -- This is why the check compares against 0 (not 1), even though
        -- the "primary_names" array starts at index 1 in Lua.
        --
        -- Note: this zero-based behavior only applies to dropdowns, not sliders.
        
        val = ui.get_int("Buybot Weapon") or 0
        if val ~= 0 then
            -- if "Buybot Weapon" returns 0, don't add the "-" to the buystring
            buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (primary[val + 1] or "") .. ";"
        end
        
        val = ui.get_int("Buybot Second") or 0
        if val ~= 0 then
            buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (secondary[val + 1] or "") .. ";"
        end
        
        val = ui.get_int("Buybot Armor") or 0
        if val ~= 0 then
            buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (equipment[val + 1] or "") .. ";"
        end
        
        val = ui.get_bool("Buy Zeus x27") or false
        if val then
            buystring = buystring .. "buy taser;"
        end
    
        -- check if the checkbox for every element of the "grenades_names" array
        -- is checked, and if so, add the buy command to the buystring.
        for i, name in pairs(grenades_names) do
            val = ui.get_bool("Buy " .. name)
            if val then
                buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (grenades[i] or "") .. ";"
            end
        end
    
        cheat.execute_command(buystring)
        
    end)

Last updated 8 months ago

# Changelog | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/changelog.md)
.

### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/changelog#october-7-2025)

October 7, 2025

*   Rearranged examples in [Quick Start](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start)
    
*   Added the [Advanced auto-buy](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start#advanced-auto-buy)
     section to [Quick Start](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start)
    
*   Added some explanations for the examples in [Quick Start](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start)
    
*   Added extra information on how to use [get\_int](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/get_int)
     and [set\_int](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/set_int)
     correctly
    
*   Added usage examples to [ui](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui)
     elements
    

* * *

### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/changelog#september-28-2025)

September 28, 2025

*   Fixed broken links in the [Quick Start](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start)
     and [Welcome!](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs)
     pages
    
*   Added links to class pages in most library pages
    
*   Added extra checks to examples so that they don't throw errors in edge cases
    

* * *

### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/changelog#july-30-2025-main-release)

July 30, 2025 - Main Release

*   The documentation is finished and ready to be used.
    

Last updated 8 months ago

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color.md). # color \`\`\`lua local clr = color.new(255, 128, 0, 200) print("Red component:", clr:r()) -- Default (0, 0, 0, 255) local a = color.new() -- RGB (alpha defaults to 255) local b = color.new(255, 128, 0) -- RGBA local c = color.new(255, 128, 0, 200) \`\`\` \`\`\`lua color.new(integer: r, integer: g, integer: b, \[integer: a\]) \`\`\` \*\*Parameters\*\*: \* \`r\` (\`integer\`): red component 0-255 \* \`g\` (\`integer\`): green component 0-255 \* \`b\` (\`integer\`): blue component 0-255 \* \`a\` (\`integer\`, optional, default: \`255\`): alpha (transparency) component 0-255

| Member | Type | Example Value |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `clr:r()` | integer | 255 |
| `clr:g()` | integer | 128 |
| `clr:b()` | integer | 0   |
| `clr:a()` | integer | 200 |

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/quick-start.md). # Quick Start ## Callbacks and drawing: \[register\\\_callback\](/docs/libraries/cheat/register\_callback.md), \[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md), \[rect\](/docs/libraries/render/rect.md) A simple showcase of how to use the rendering and color APIs. \`\`\`lua -- draw callbacks run every frame cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function() local clr = color.new(255, 0, 0, 255) -- create a new color render.rect(100, 100, 50, 50, clr) -- and use it to render a red rectangle -- at x=100, y=100, size: 50x50 px end) \`\`\` ## Kill say \[register\\\_callback\](/docs/libraries/cheat/register\_callback.md), \[execute\\\_command\](/docs/libraries/cheat/execute\_command.md), \[game\\\_event\](/docs/classes/game\_event.md), \[get\\\_entity\\\_from\\\_user\\\_id\](/docs/libraries/entities/get\_entity\_from\_user\_id.md), \[player\](/docs/classes/player.md) Say a message when you kill an enemy or vice versa. \`\`\`lua local function killsay(event) local kill = "ez" local death = "lucky" local victim = entities.get\_entity\_from\_user\_id(event:get\_int("userid")) local attacker = entities.get\_entity\_from\_user\_id(event:get\_int("attacker")) if not victim then return -- check if the victim is a player end if not attacker then return -- check if the attacker is a player end if victim:is\_local\_player() then -- if the local player dies cheat.execute\_command("say " .. death) elseif attacker:is\_local\_player() then -- if a player is killed by local player cheat.execute\_command("say " .. kill) end end -- game event callbacks run when game events occur cheat.register\_callback("player\_death", killsay) \`\`\` ## Simple auto-buy \[register\\\_callback\](/docs/libraries/cheat/register\_callback.md), \[execute\\\_command\](/docs/libraries/cheat/execute\_command.md), \[game\\\_event\](/docs/classes/game\_event.md) A simple automatic buybot that executes on the start of a new round. \`\`\`lua cheat.register\_callback("round\_prestart", function() -- multi-line string cheat.execute\_command(\[\[buy scar20; buy deagle; buy vest; buy vesthelm; buy incgrenade; buy molotov; buy hegrenade; buy smokegrenade\]\]) end) \`\`\` ## Menu elements \[ui\](/docs/libraries/ui.md), \[register\\\_callback\](/docs/libraries/cheat/register\_callback.md) A simple checkbox and slider to showcase how the UI API is used. \`\`\`lua ui.add\_checkbox("Check me!") ui.add\_slider\_int("Drag me!", 1, 10) cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function() if ui.get\_bool("Check me!") then -- check the value of the checkbox -- if "Check me!" is checked (and get\_bool() returns "true", -- print the value of the "Drag me!" slider. print("I'm checked and my slider value is " .. tostring(ui.get\_int("Drag me!")) .. "!") end end) \`\`\` ## Advanced auto-buy \[register\\\_callback\](/docs/libraries/cheat/register\_callback.md), \[ui\](/docs/libraries/ui.md), \[execute\\\_command\](/docs/libraries/cheat/execute\_command.md), \[game\\\_event\](/docs/classes/game\_event.md) A more advanced automatic buybot that allows you to select which weapons to buy via the UI and runs the command on the start of a new round. \`\`\`lua local primary = {"", "ak47","ssg08","sg556","awp","scar20","galilar","mac10","mp7","ump45","p90","bizon","nova","xm1014","mag7","m249","negev"} local primary\_names = {"-", "AK-47 / M4A4 / M4A1-S","SSG 08","SG 553 / AUG","AWP","G3SG1 / SCAR-20","Galil AR / Famas","MAC-10 / MP9","MP7 / MP5-SD","UMP-45","P90","PP-Bizon","Nova","XM1014","Sawed-Off / MAG-7","M249","Negev"} local secondary = {"", "glock","elite","p250","tec9","deagle"} local secondary\_names = {"-", "Glock-18 / USP-S / P2000","Dual Berettas","P250","Tec-9 / Five-Seven","Desert Eagle / Revolver"} local equipment = {"", "vest","vesthelm"} local equipment\_names = { "-", "Kevlar Vest","Kevlar + Helmet"} local grenades = {"molotov","decoy","flashbang","flashbang","hegrenade","smokegrenade"} local grenades\_names = {"Molotov / Incendiary Grenade","Decoy Grenade","Flashbang 1","Flashbang 2","HE Grenade","Smoke Grenade"} -- create all of the UI elements ui.add\_checkbox("Enable Buybot") ui.add\_dropdown("Buybot Weapon", primary\_names) ui.add\_dropdown("Buybot Second", secondary\_names) ui.add\_dropdown("Buybot Armor", equipment\_names) ui.add\_checkbox("Buy Zeus x27") for i, name in pairs(grenades\_names) do ui.add\_checkbox("Buy " .. name) end cheat.register\_callback("round\_prestart", function() if not ui.get\_bool("Enable Buybot") then return end local buystring = "" local val = 0 -- IMPORTANT: -- the get\_int() function returns the selected item index as a zero-based value. -- This means the first element is indexed as 0 (C-style), not 1 (Lua-style)! -- -- In Lua, arrays start at index 1, so you should always add +1 to the value -- returned by get\_int() when working with dropdowns. -- -- Example: -- If get\_int() returns 0, it means the first item is selected. -- To access the correct element in a Lua table, use: -- primary\[val + 1\] -- -- This is why the check compares against 0 (not 1), even though -- the "primary\_names" array starts at index 1 in Lua. -- -- Note: this zero-based behavior only applies to dropdowns, not sliders. val = ui.get\_int("Buybot Weapon") or 0 if val ~= 0 then -- if "Buybot Weapon" returns 0, don't add the "-" to the buystring buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (primary\[val + 1\] or "") .. ";" end val = ui.get\_int("Buybot Second") or 0 if val ~= 0 then buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (secondary\[val + 1\] or "") .. ";" end val = ui.get\_int("Buybot Armor") or 0 if val ~= 0 then buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (equipment\[val + 1\] or "") .. ";" end val = ui.get\_bool("Buy Zeus x27") or false if val then buystring = buystring .. "buy taser;" end -- check if the checkbox for every element of the "grenades\_names" array -- is checked, and if so, add the buy command to the buystring. for i, name in pairs(grenades\_names) do val = ui.get\_bool("Buy " .. name) if val then buystring = buystring .. "buy " .. (grenades\[i\] or "") .. ";" end end cheat.execute\_command(buystring) end) \`\`\` --- # Agent Instructions This documentation is published with GitBook. GitBook is the documentation platform designed so that both humans and AI agents can read, navigate, and reason over technical content effectively. # is_key_pressed | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/input/is_key_pressed.md)
.

Copy

    local pressed = input.is_key_pressed(key)

Returns a `boolean` value that is `true` if the key specified is pressed.

**Parameters:**

*   `key` (`integer`): a key code from the table below
    

**Returns:**

*   `boolean`

1

Right mouse button

(Undefined / Reserved)

9

(Undefined)

14–15

18

28

# get_server_string | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/world/get_server_string.md)
.

Copy

    local server = world.get_server_string()

Retrieves the currently joined server's address. Returns `unknown` if the player is not connected to a server. Returns `local server` if the player is connected to a local server.

**Returns:**

*   `string`

.

Copy

    cheat.unregister_callback(event_id)

Unregister a callback.

The currently available callback events are:

*   PreDraw
    
*   Draw
    
*   CreateMove
    
*   FrameStageNotify
    
*   Unload
    
*   VoiceData
    
*   Game Events ([click here](https://wiki.alliedmods.net/Counter-Strike:_Global_Offensive_Events)
    )
    

**Parameters:**

*   `event_id` (`string`): a callback event ID.

# register_callback | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/register_callback.md)
.

Copy

    cheat.register_callback(event_id, func)
    
    -- example using built-in event
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
        print("Hello World") -- prints text every frame
    end)
    
    -- use game event instead of built-in event
    cheat.register_callback("weapon_fire", function(event)
        local weapon_name = event:get_string("weapon")
        print(weapon_name)
    end)
    
    -- example without in-line functions
    local function run_event(event)
        local item = event:get_string("item")
        print("someone picked up " .. item)
    end
    
    cheat.register_callback("item_pickup", run_event)

Register an event callback. Used for running code when something happens in-game (bomb is planted, new round starts, player dies etc.)

The currently available callback events are:

*   PreDraw
    
*   Draw
    
*   CreateMove
    
*   FrameStageNotify
    
*   Unload
    
*   VoiceData
    
*   Game Events ([click here](https://wiki.alliedmods.net/Counter-Strike:_Global_Offensive_Events)
    )
    

**Parameters:**

*   `event_id` (`string`): a callback event ID.
    
*   `func` (`function`): a function to execute on the execution of the specified event.
    

Last updated 8 months ago

---

# line | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/trace/line.md)
.

Copy

    local trace_data = trace.line(startpos, endpos, mask, [skip])

Trace a line in the game world.

**Parameters:**

*   `startpos` ([vector](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector)
    ): the starting 3D position of the trace.
    
*   `endpos` ([vector](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector)
    ): the ending 3D position of the trace.
    
*   `mask` (`integer`): the [trace mask](https://github.com/ValveSoftware/source-sdk-2013/blob/0d8dceea4310fde5706b3ce1c70609d72a38efdf/sp/src/public/bspflags.h#L104)
    .
    
*   `skip` ([player](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/player)
    , optional)
    

**Returns:**

*   [trace\_data](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/trace_data)
    

For more information about TraceData, please read [https://developer.valvesoftware.com/wiki/UTIL\_TraceLine#trace\_t\_.26tr](https://developer.valvesoftware.com/wiki/UTIL_TraceLine#trace_t_.26tr)

Last updated 10 months ago

# send_data | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/utils/send_data.md)
.

Copy

    utils.send_data(bits)

Sends raw data through a custom network buffer (used in exploits/hv packets/etc).

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/utils/send_data#parameters)

**Parameters:**

*   `bits` (`uint64_t`): data to send.
    

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/utils/send_data#notes)

Notes:

*   Make sure the server supports or expects this, or it may result in a kick.

# find_signature | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/utils/find_signature.md)
.

Copy

    utils.find_signature(module, signature)

Finds a memory address using a signature scan.

**Returns:**

*   `module` (`string`):name of the module (`client.dll`, etc).
    
*   `signature` (`string`): IDA-style pattern (e.g. `"55 8B ?? EC 83 EC"`).
    

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/utils/find_signature#returns)

**Returns:**

*   `uintptr_t`: pointer to the interface.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# voice_packet | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/voice_packet.md)
.

Copy

    cheat.register_callback("VoiceData", function(packet)
        print("Voice data from entity: " .. tostring(packet:entity()))
        print("Data length: " .. #packet:bits())
    end)
    

Member

Type

Description

`bits`

`string`

Raw encoded voice data as a string (likely binary or compressed)

`entity`

`entity`

Entity that belongs to the voice packet.

`xuid_low`

`uint32_t`

Lower 32 bits of the player's XUID

`xuid_high`

`uint32_t`

Upper 32 bits of the player's XUID

`section_number`

`uint32_t`

Voice stream section number (useful for packet ordering)

`uncompressed_sample_offset`

`uint32_t`

Sample offset in the full uncompressed stream

`sequence_bytes`

`uint32_t`

Packet sequence bytes

`format`

`int32_t`

Audio encoding format ID (engine-specific)

Last updated 10 months ago

# set_view_angles | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/usercmd/set_view_angles.md)
.

Copy

    usercmd.set_view_angles(vec, silent)

Sets the command’s view angles.

**Parameters:**

*   `vec` ([vector](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector)
    ): desired view angles.
    
*   `silent` (`bool`, optional): if `true`, angle won't visually apply to player (silent aimbot).
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# game_event | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/game_event.md)
.

Copy

    cheat.register_callback("player_death", function(event)
        local userid = event:get_int("userid") -- get the userid of the victim
        event:set_bool("headshot", true) -- show a fake headshot icon in the killfeed
        local distance = event:get_float("distance") -- distance to the victim
    end)

A list of game events and their structure information can be found [here](https://wiki.alliedmods.net/Counter-Strike:_Global_Offensive_Events)
.

Member

Return Type

Example Value

get\_bool

boolean

Copy

    true

get\_int

integer

Copy

    2

get\_float

float

Copy

    2.f

get\_string

string

Copy

    "weapon_ak47"

Member

Expected Type

Example

set\_bool

boolean

Copy

    event:set_bool("headshot", true)

set\_int

integer

Copy

    event:set_int("userid", 10)

set\_float

float

Copy

    event:set_float("distance", 5.2)

set\_string

string

Copy

    event:set_string("weapon", "weapon_scar20")

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# entity | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/entity.md)
.

Copy

    local me = entities.get_local_player()
    print(me:get_prop_int("DT_BaseEntity", "m_iTeamNum"))
    
    if me:get_prop_bool("DT_BaseEntity", "m_bSpotted") then
        print("I'm spotted!")
    end
    
    local_player:set_prop_int("DT_BaseEntity", "m_iTeamNum", 2)

Check the [props list](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/entity/props-list)
 for more information on available entity props.

Function

Syntax

get\_prop\_int

Copy

    ent:get_prop_int(string: table, string: var)

get\_prop\_float

Copy

    ent:get_prop_float(string: table, string: var)

get\_prop\_bool

Copy

    ent:get_prop_bool(string: table, string: var)

get\_prop\_string

Copy

    ent:get_prop_string(string: table, string: var)

Function

Syntax

set\_prop\_int

Copy

    ent:set_prop_int(string: table, string: var, integer: value)

set\_prop\_float

Copy

    ent:set_prop_float(string: table, string: var, float: value)

set\_prop\_bool

Copy

    ent:set_prop_bool(string: table, string: var, boolean: value)

Last updated 10 months ago

.

Copy

    local me = entities.get_local_player()

Returns the local player's `Player` class, or `nil` if not in-game.

**Returns:**

*   [player](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/player)
    : the local player object.

# rect_filled | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/rect_filled.md)
.

Copy

    render.rect_filled(x, y, width, height, color, [rounding])

Draws a filled rectangle.

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the x-coordinate of the top-left corner.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the y-coordinate of the top-left corner.
    
*   `width` (`float`): the width of the rectangle.
    
*   `height` (`float`): the height of the rectangle.
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): the fill color.
    
*   `rounding` (`float`, optional): rounds the corners of the rectangle. Defaults to `0.0`.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

# rect | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/rect.md)
.

Copy

    render.rect(x, y, width, height, color, [thickness], [rounding])

Draws an outlined rectangle at the specified position.

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the x-coordinate of the top-left corner.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the y-coordinate of the top-left corner.
    
*   `width` (`float`): the width of the rectangle.
    
*   `height` (`float`): the height of the rectangle.
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): the outline color.
    
*   `thickness` (`float`, optional): the line thickness. Defaults to `1.0`.
    
*   `rounding` (`float`, optional): rounds the corners of the rectangle. Defaults to `0.0`.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# text | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/text.md)
.

Copy

    render.text(x, y, text, size, color, font, [center], [outline])

Draws a string of text on the screen at the specified coordinates using a custom font and rendering options.

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the horizontal position on the screen.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the vertical position on the screen.
    
*   `text` (`string`): the text to render.
    
*   `size` (`float`): the font size for the text.
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): the color to render the text in.
    
*   `font` (`Font`): the font object used to draw the text. Must be loaded. See [add\_font](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/add_font)
    
*   `center` (`bool`, optional): if `true`, centers the text horizontally. Defaults to `false`.
    
*   `outline` (`bool`, optional): if `true`, renders an outline around the text. Defaults to `false`.
    

**Notes:**

*   If the `font` is `nil` or not loaded, nothing will be drawn.
    

Last updated 8 months ago

---

# filled_circle | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/filled_circle.md)
.

Copy

    render.filled_circle(x, y, radius, points, color)

Draws a filled circle at the specified position with the given radius and color.

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the horizontal screen coordinate of the circle center.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the vertical screen coordinate of the circle center.
    
*   `radius` (`float`): the radius of the circle.
    
*   `points` (`int`): the number of segments used to draw the circle (higher = smoother).
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): the fill color of the circle.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# line | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/line.md)
.

Copy

    render.line(x, y, x1, y1, color, [thickness])

Draws a straight line between two points on the screen using the specified color and optional thickness.

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/line#parameters)

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the starting point’s horizontal screen coordinate.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the starting point’s vertical screen coordinate.
    
*   `x1` (`float`): the ending point’s horizontal screen coordinate.
    
*   `y1` (`float`): the ending point’s vertical screen coordinate.
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): the color to render the line in.
    
*   `thickness` (`float`, optional): the thickness of the line. Defaults to `1.0`.
    

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/line#notes)

**Notes:**

*   If `thickness` is not provided, the line will be drawn with a default thickness of `1.0`.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# polygon | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/polygon.md)
.

Copy

    render.polygon(pos1, pos2, pos3, color)

Draws a filled triangle (polygon) between three 2D points.

**Parameters:**

*   `pos1` ([vector2d](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector2d)
    ): first point of the triangle.
    
*   `pos2` ([vector2d](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector2d)
    ): second point of the triangle.
    
*   `pos3` ([vector2d](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector2d)
    ): third point of the triangle.
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): fill color of the triangle.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

# world_to_screen | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/world_to_screen.md)
.

Copy

    render.world_to_screen(world_pos)

Converts a 3D world position to a 2D screen position.

**Parameters:**

*   `world_pos` ([vector](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector)
    ): the 3D position in the world.
    

**Returns:**

*   [vector2d](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/vector2d)
    : the corresponding 2D screen coordinates.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# arc | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/arc.md)
.

Copy

    render.arc(x, y, radius, points, start_angle, end_angle, color, [thickness])

Draws an arc of a circle between two angles.

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the x-coordinate of the circle center.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the y-coordinate of the circle center.
    
*   `radius` (`float`): the radius of the arc.
    
*   `points` (`int`): the number of segments (smoother = higher).
    
*   `start_angle` (`float`): starting angle in radians.
    
*   `end_angle` (`float`): ending angle in radians.
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): the color of the arc.
    
*   `thickness` (`float`, optional): line thickness. Defaults to `1.0`.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

---

# circle | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/circle.md)
.

Copy

    render.circle(x, y, radius, points, color)

Draws an outlined circle at the specified position with the given radius and color.

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the horizontal screen coordinate of the circle center.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the vertical screen coordinate of the circle center.
    
*   `radius` (`float`): the radius of the circle.
    
*   `points` (`int`): the number of segments used to draw the circle.
    
*   `color` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): the outline color of the circle.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

# gradient_rect | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/gradient_rect.md)
.

Copy

    render.gradient_rect(x, y, width, height, horizontal, color1, color2)

Draws a gradient-filled rectangle.

**Parameters:**

*   `x` (`float`): the x-coordinate of the top-left corner.
    
*   `y` (`float`): the y-coordinate of the top-left corner.
    
*   `width` (`float`): width of the rectangle.
    
*   `height` (`float`): height of the rectangle.
    
*   `horizontal` (`bool`): direction of the gradient (`true` for left-right, `false` for top-bottom).
    
*   `color1` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): starting color.
    
*   `color2` ([color](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/color)
    ): ending color.
    

Last updated 10 months ago

# player | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/player.md)
.

Example usage:

Copy

    cheat.register_callback("player_death", function(event)
    
        local victim = entities.get_entity_from_user_id(event:get_int("userid"))
        local attacker = entities.get_entity_from_user_id(event:get_int("attacker"))
        
        if not attacker and not victim then
            return
        end
        
        if not attacker then
            if victim:IsLocalPlayer() then
                print("You just killed yourself! 🚑")
            end
        else
            if attacker:IsLocalPlayer() then
                print("You just killed " .. victim:GetName() .. "!")
            elseif victim:IsLocalPlayer() then
                print("Uh-oh! You were killed by " .. attacker:GetName() .. "!"
            end
        end
    
    end)

# frametime | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/globals/frametime.md)
.

Copy

    local delta = globals.frametime()
    
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
    
        delta = globals.frametime()
        -- delta = 1.0 / globals.framerate() -- this achieves the same result
        print("Time since last frame: " .. delta .. "ms")
    
    end)

Returns the time that has passed since the last frame. Calculated using the formula `delta = 1.0 / FPS`

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/globals/frametime#returns)

Returns:


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

`float`: frame time.

Last updated 8 months ago

---

# set_int | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/set_int.md)
.

Copy

    ui.set_int(name, value)

Sets the integer value of an integer slider or dropdown.

**Parameters:**

*   `name` (`string`): unique identifier of the integer slider/dropdown.
    
*   `value` (`integer`):
    
    *   when used with [add\_slider\_int](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_slider_int)
        , this is the numerical value to set.
        
    *   When used with [add\_dropdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_dropdown)
        , this is the zero-based index of the option to select. The first option has index `0`, the second has index `1`, and so on.
        
    

Last updated 8 months ago

---

# add_slider_float | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_slider_float.md)
.

Copy

    ui.add_slider_float(name, min, max)

Adds a float-based slider input.

**Parameters:**

*   `name` (`string`): unique identifier.
    
*   `min` (`float`): minimum value.
    
*   `max` (`float`): maximum value.
    

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_slider_float#notes)

Notes:

*   Selected index can be retrieved via [get\_float](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/get_float)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_slider_float#example)

Example

Copy

    ui.add_slider_float("Drag me!", 1.0, 10.0)
    
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
        local slider_value = ui.get_float("Drag me!")
        print("The slider value is " .. tostring(slider_value) .. "!")
    end)

Last updated 8 months ago

---

# add_checkbox | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_checkbox.md)
.

Copy

    ui.add_checkbox(name)

Adds a checkbox to the menu.

**Parameters:**

*   `name` (`string`): identifier/label for the checkbox.
    

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_checkbox#notes)

Notes:

*   Value can be accessed with [get\_bool](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/get_bool)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_checkbox#example)

Example:

Print "I'm checked!" every frame the checkbox is checked.

Copy

    ui.add_checkbox("Check me!")
    
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
        if ui.get_bool("Check me!") then
            print("I'm checked!")
        end
    end)

Last updated 8 months ago

# add_dropdown | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_dropdown.md)
.

Copy

    ui.add_dropdown(name, labels)

Creates a dropdown with predefined label options.

**Parameters:**

*   `name` (`string`): identifier for the dropdown.
    
*   `labels` (`table`): lua array of string options.
    

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_dropdown#notes)

Notes:

*   Selected index can be retrieved via [get\_int](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/get_int)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_dropdown#example)

Example

Copy

    local items = { "apple", "banana", "orange", "cherry" }
    ui.add_dropdown("Items", items)
    
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
        local current_item = ui.get_int("Items") + 1
        print("The currently selected item is " .. items[current_item])
    end)

Last updated 8 months ago

---

# add_slider_int | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_slider_int.md)
.

Copy

    ui.add_slider_int(name, min, max)

Adds an integer slider input.

**Parameters:**

*   `name` (`string`): unique identifier.
    
*   `min` (`integer`): minimum value.
    
*   `max` (`integer`): maximum value.
    

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_slider_int#notes)

Notes:

*   Selected index can be retrieved via [get\_int](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/get_int)
    .
    

* * *

#### 

[](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add_slider_int#example)

Example

Copy

    ui.add_slider_int("Drag me!", 1, 10)
    
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
        local slider_value = ui.get_int("Drag me!")
        print("The slider value is " .. tostring(slider_value) .. "!")
    end)

Copy

    local max_slider = 250
    local min_slider = 1
    local right = true
    ui.add_slider_int("Watch me!", min_slider, max_slider)
    
    cheat.register_callback("Draw", function()
    
        local slider_value = ui.get_int("Watch me!")
        
        if right then
            if slider_value < max_slider then
                slider_value = slider_value + 1
            elseif slider_value == max_slider then
                right = false
            end
        else
            if slider_value > min_slider then
                slider_value = slider_value - 1
            elseif slider_value == min_slider then
                right = true
            end
        end
        
        ui.set_int("Watch me!", slider_value)
        
    end)

Last updated 8 months ago

# get\\\_cursor\\\_position

\`\`\`lua
local cpos = input.get\_cursor\_position()
\`\`\`

Retrieves the mouse cursor/pointer position.

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \[vector2d\](/docs/classes/vector2d.md)

# is\\\_key\\\_pressed

\`\`\`lua
local pressed = input.is\_key\_pressed(key)
\`\`\`

Returns a \`boolean\` value that is \`true\` if the key specified is pressed.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`key\` (\`integer\`): a key code from the table below

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \`boolean\`

| Key Name                                           | Value   |
| -------------------------------------------------- | ------- |
| Left mouse button                                  | 1       |
| Right mouse button                                 | 2       |
| Control‑Break processing                           | 3       |
| Middle mouse button                                | 4       |
| X1 mouse button                                    | 5       |
| X2 mouse button                                    | 6       |
| (Undefined / Reserved)                             | 7       |
| Backspace                                          | 8       |
| Tab                                                | 9       |
| (Reserved / Undefined)                             | 10–11   |
| Clear                                              | 12      |
| Enter (Return)                                     | 13      |
| (Undefined)                                        | 14–15   |
| Shift                                              | 16      |
| Ctrl                                               | 17      |
| Alt                                                | 18      |
| Pause                                              | 19      |
| Caps Lock                                          | 20      |
| IME Kana/Hangul mode                               | 21      |
| (Undefined)                                        | 22      |
| IME Junja mode                                     | 23      |
| IME Final mode                                     | 24      |
| IME Hanja/Kanji mode                               | 25      |
| (Undefined)                                        | 26      |

# get\\\_map\\\_name

\`\`\`lua
local map\_name = world.get\_map\_name()
\`\`\`

Retrieve the current short map name.

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \`string\`: the short map name as a \`string\` value.&#x20;

{% hint style="info" %}
This function is identical to \[get\\\_level\\\_name\\\_short\](/docs/libraries/engine/get\_level\_name\_short.md)
{% endhint %}

# weapon

cheat.print(message)

# get\\\_server\\\_string

\`\`\`lua
local server = world.get\_server\_string()
\`\`\`

Retrieves the currently joined server's address. Returns \`unknown\` if the player is not connected to a server. Returns \`local server\` if the player is connected to a local server.

# unregister\\\_callback

\`\`\`lua
cheat.unregister\_callback(event\_id)
\`\`\`

Unregister a callback.

{% hint style="info" %}
The currently available callback events are:

\* PreDraw
\* Draw
\* CreateMove
\* FrameStageNotify
\* Unload
\* VoiceData
\* Game Events (\[click here\](https://wiki.alliedmods.net/Counter-Strike:\_Global\_Offensive\_Events))
  {% endhint %}

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`event\_id\` (\`string\`): a callback event ID.


---

# rect

\`\`\`lua
render.rect(x, y, width, height, color, \[thickness\], \[rounding\])
\`\`\`

Draws an outlined rectangle at the specified position.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the x-coordinate of the top-left corner.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the y-coordinate of the top-left corner.
\* \`width\` (\`float\`): the width of the rectangle.
\* \`height\` (\`float\`): the height of the rectangle.
\* \`color\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): the outline color.
\* \`thickness\` (\`float\`, optional): the line thickness. Defaults to \`1.0\`.
\* \`rounding\` (\`float\`, optional): rounds the corners of the rectangle. Defaults to \`0.0\`.


---

# line

\`\`\`lua
local trace\_data = trace.line(startpos, endpos, mask, \[skip\])
\`\`\`

Trace a line in the game world.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`startpos\` (\[vector\](/docs/classes/vector.md)): the starting 3D position of the trace.
\* \`endpos\` (\[vector\](/docs/classes/vector.md)): the ending 3D position of the trace.
\* \`mask\` (\`integer\`): the \[trace mask\](https://github.com/ValveSoftware/source-sdk-2013/blob/0d8dceea4310fde5706b3ce1c70609d72a38efdf/sp/src/public/bspflags.h#L104).
\* \`skip\` (\[player\](/docs/classes/player.md), optional)

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \[trace\\\_data\](/docs/classes/trace\_data.md)

{% hint style="info" %}
For more information about TraceData, please read <https://developer.valvesoftware.com/wiki/UTIL\_TraceLine#trace\_t\_.26tr>
{% endhint %}

# add\\\_slider\\\_int

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_slider\_int(name, min, max)
\`\`\`

Adds an integer slider input.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`name\` (\`string\`): unique identifier.
\* \`min\` (\`integer\`): minimum value.
\* \`max\` (\`integer\`): maximum value.

#### Notes:

\* Selected index can be retrieved via \[get\\\_int\](/docs/libraries/ui/get\_int.md).

\*\*\*

#### Example

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_slider\_int("Drag me!", 1, 10)

cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function()
    local slider\_value = ui.get\_int("Drag me!")
    print("The slider value is " .. tostring(slider\_value) .. "!")
end)
\`\`\`

\`\`\`lua
local max\_slider = 250
local min\_slider = 1
local right = true
ui.add\_slider\_int("Watch me!", min\_slider, max\_slider)

cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function()

    local slider\_value = ui.get\_int("Watch me!")
    
    if right then
        if slider\_value < max\_slider then
            slider\_value = slider\_value + 1
        elseif slider\_value == max\_slider then
            right = false
        end
    else
        if slider\_value > min\_slider then
            slider\_value = slider\_value - 1
        elseif slider\_value == min\_slider then
            right = true
        end
    end
    
    ui.set\_int("Watch me!", slider\_value)
    
end)
\`\`\`


---

# set\\\_int

\`\`\`lua
ui.set\_int(name, value)
\`\`\`

Sets the integer value of an integer slider or dropdown.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`name\` (\`string\`): unique identifier of the integer slider/dropdown.
\* \`value\` (\`integer\`):
  \* when used with \[add\\\_slider\\\_int\](/docs/libraries/ui/add\_slider\_int.md), this is the numerical value to set.
  \* When used with \[add\\\_dropdown\](/docs/libraries/ui/add\_dropdown.md), this is the zero-based index of the option to select.\\
    The first option has index \`0\`, the second has index \`1\`, and so on.


---

# add\\\_dropdown

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_dropdown(name, labels)
\`\`\`

Creates a dropdown with predefined label options.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`name\` (\`string\`): identifier for the dropdown.
\* \`labels\` (\`table\`): lua array of string options.

#### Notes:

\* Selected index can be retrieved via \[get\\\_int\](/docs/libraries/ui/get\_int.md).

\*\*\*

#### Example

\`\`\`lua
local items = { "apple", "banana", "orange", "cherry" }
ui.add\_dropdown("Items", items)

cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function()
    local current\_item = ui.get\_int("Items") + 1
    print("The currently selected item is " .. items\[current\_item\])
end)
\`\`\`


---

# add\\\_slider\\\_float

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_slider\_float(name, min, max)
\`\`\`

Adds a float-based slider input.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`name\` (\`string\`): unique identifier.
\* \`min\` (\`float\`): minimum value.
\* \`max\` (\`float\`): maximum value.

#### Notes:

\* Selected index can be retrieved via \[get\\\_float\](/docs/libraries/ui/get\_float.md).

\*\*\*

#### Example

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_slider\_float("Drag me!", 1.0, 10.0)

cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function()
    local slider\_value = ui.get\_float("Drag me!")
    print("The slider value is " .. tostring(slider\_value) .. "!")
end)
\`\`\`


---

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/text.md).

# text

\`\`\`lua
render.text(x, y, text, size, color, font, \[center\], \[outline\])
\`\`\`

Draws a string of text on the screen at the specified coordinates using a custom font and rendering options.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the horizontal position on the screen.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the vertical position on the screen.
\* \`text\` (\`string\`): the text to render.
\* \`size\` (\`float\`): the font size for the text.
\* \`color\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): the color to render the text in.
\* \`font\` (\`Font\`): the font object used to draw the text. Must be loaded. See \[add\\\_font\](/docs/libraries/render/add\_font.md)
\* \`center\` (\`bool\`, optional): if \`true\`, centers the text horizontally. Defaults to \`false\`.
\* \`outline\` (\`bool\`, optional): if \`true\`, renders an outline around the text. Defaults to \`false\`.

\*\*Notes:\*\*

\* If the \`font\` is \`nil\` or not loaded, nothing will be drawn.


---

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/arc.md).

# arc

\`\`\`lua
render.arc(x, y, radius, points, start\_angle, end\_angle, color, \[thickness\])
\`\`\`

Draws an arc of a circle between two angles.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the x-coordinate of the circle center.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the y-coordinate of the circle center.
\* \`radius\` (\`float\`): the radius of the arc.
\* \`points\` (\`int\`): the number of segments (smoother = higher).
\* \`start\_angle\` (\`float\`): starting angle in radians.
\* \`end\_angle\` (\`float\`): ending angle in radians.
\* \`color\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): the color of the arc.
\* \`thickness\` (\`float\`, optional): line thickness. Defaults to \`1.0\`.


---

# plane

\`\`\`lua
local plane = trace:plane()
print("Normal:", plane:normal())
\`\`\`

| Member   | Type                              | Example Value   |
| -------- | --------------------------------- | --------------- |
| normal   | \[vector\](/docs/classes/vector.md) | {0.0, 0.0, 1.0} |
| dist     | float                             | 12.5            |
| type     | integer                           | 5               |
| signbits | integer                           | 2               |

# add\\\_font

\`\`\`lua
render.add\_font(path, size)
\`\`\`

Loads and registers a font from a \`.ttf\` file.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`path\` (\`string\`): path to the \`.ttf\` font file.
\* \`size\` (\`int\`): size of the font to load.

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \`Font\`: a font object that can be used in rendering functions (e.g., \`render.text\`).

# filled\\\_circle

\`\`\`lua
render.filled\_circle(x, y, radius, points, color)
\`\`\`

Draws a filled circle at the specified position with the given radius and color.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the horizontal screen coordinate of the circle center.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the vertical screen coordinate of the circle center.
\* \`radius\` (\`float\`): the radius of the circle.
\* \`points\` (\`int\`): the number of segments used to draw the circle (higher = smoother).
\* \`color\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): the fill color of the circle.

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/line.md).

# line

\`\`\`lua
render.line(x, y, x1, y1, color, \[thickness\])
\`\`\`

Draws a straight line between two points on the screen using the specified color and optional thickness.

#### \*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the starting point’s horizontal screen coordinate.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the starting point’s vertical screen coordinate.
\* \`x1\` (\`float\`): the ending point’s horizontal screen coordinate.
\* \`y1\` (\`float\`): the ending point’s vertical screen coordinate.
\* \`color\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): the color to render the line in.
\* \`thickness\` (\`float\`, optional): the thickness of the line. Defaults to \`1.0\`.

#### \*\*Notes:\*\*

\* If \`thickness\` is not provided, the line will be drawn with a default thickness of \`1.0\`.


---

render.polygon(pos1, pos2, pos3, color)

# gradient\\\_rect

\`\`\`lua
render.gradient\_rect(x, y, width, height, horizontal, color1, color2)
\`\`\`

Draws a gradient-filled rectangle.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the x-coordinate of the top-left corner.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the y-coordinate of the top-left corner.
\* \`width\` (\`float\`): width of the rectangle.
\* \`height\` (\`float\`): height of the rectangle.
\* \`horizontal\` (\`bool\`): direction of the gradient (\`true\` for left-right, \`false\` for top-bottom).
\* \`color1\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): starting color.
\* \`color2\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): ending color.


---

# get\\\_int

\`\`\`lua
ui.get\_int(name)
\`\`\`

Gets the integer value of an integer slider or dropdown.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`name\` (\`string\`): unique identifier of the integer slider or dropdown.

#### Returns:

\* \`integer\`:
  \* when used with \[add\\\_slider\\\_int\](/docs/libraries/ui/add\_slider\_int.md), returns the current numerical value
  \* when used with \[add\\\_dropdown\](/docs/libraries/ui/add\_dropdown.md), returns the zero-based index of the currently selected option.\\
    The first option has index \`0\`, the second has index \`1\`, and so on.


---

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/player.md).

# player

Example usage:

\`\`\`lua
cheat.register\_callback("player\_death", function(event)

    local victim = entities.get\_entity\_from\_user\_id(event:get\_int("userid"))
    local attacker = entities.get\_entity\_from\_user\_id(event:get\_int("attacker"))
    
    if not attacker and not victim then
        return
    end
    
    if not attacker then
        if victim:IsLocalPlayer() then
            print("You just killed yourself! 🚑")
        end
    else
        if attacker:IsLocalPlayer() then
            print("You just killed " .. victim:GetName() .. "!")
        elseif victim:IsLocalPlayer() then
            print("Uh-oh! You were killed by " .. attacker:GetName() .. "!"
        end
    end

end)
\`\`\`

# get\\\_enemies

\`\`\`lua
local enemies = entities.get\_enemies()
\`\`\`

Returns all enemy players.

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* List of \[player\](/docs/classes/player.md) objects currently on the enemy team as a \`table\`.

# get\\\_entity\\\_by\\\_index

\`\`\`lua
local enemy = entities.get\_entity\_by\_index(index)
\`\`\`

Returns the player at the specified index in the entity list.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`index\` (\`integer\`): the index of a player in the entity list.

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \[player\](/docs/classes/player.md): the player object at \`index\`.

# next\\\_line

\`\`\`lua
ui.next\_line()
\`\`\`

Inserts a vertical spacing offset between UI elements.

\*\*\*

#### Example:

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_checkbox("Checkbox 1")
ui.next\_line()
ui.add\_slider\_int("Slider 1", 1, 10)
\`\`\`

# entity

\`\`\`lua
local me = entities.get\_local\_player()
print(me:get\_prop\_int("DT\_BaseEntity", "m\_iTeamNum"))

if me:get\_prop\_bool("DT\_BaseEntity", "m\_bSpotted") then
    print("I'm spotted!")
end

local\_player:set\_prop\_int("DT\_BaseEntity", "m\_iTeamNum", 2)
\`\`\`

# player\\\_info

\`\`\`lua
local local\_idx = engine.get\_local\_player\_index()
local info = engine.get\_player\_info(local\_idx)

print(info:name())

if info:bot() then
    print("This is a bot!")
end
\`\`\`

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/render/circle.md).

# circle

\`\`\`lua
render.circle(x, y, radius, points, color)
\`\`\`

Draws an outlined circle at the specified position with the given radius and color.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the horizontal screen coordinate of the circle center.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the vertical screen coordinate of the circle center.
\* \`radius\` (\`float\`): the radius of the circle.
\* \`points\` (\`int\`): the number of segments used to draw the circle.
\* \`color\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): the outline color of the circle.


---

# trace\\\_data

\`\`\`lua
local trace\_data = trace.line(vecstart, vecend, 0xFFFFFFFF)

if trace\_data:hit\_entity() then
    print("We hit something!")
end
\`\`\`

{% hint style="info" %}
For more information about TraceData, please read <https://developer.valvesoftware.com/wiki/UTIL\_TraceLine#trace\_t\_.26tr>

\\
For trace masks, please refer to <https://github.com/ValveSoftware/source-sdk-2013/blob/0d8dceea4310fde5706b3ce1c70609d72a38efdf/sp/src/public/bspflags.h#L104>
{% endhint %}

| Member                | Type                              | Example Value                  |
| --------------------- | --------------------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| allsolid              | boolean                           | false                          |
| contents              | integer                           | 1073741825                     |
| dispflags             | integer                           | 0                              |
| endpos                | \[vector\](/docs/classes/vector.md) | {100.0, 50.0, 0.0}             |
| fraction              | float                             | 0.82                           |
| fraction\\\_left\\\_solid | float                             | 0.0                            |
| hitbox                | integer                           | 5                              |
| hitgroup              | integer                           | 1                              |
| hit\\\_entity           | \[entity\](/docs/classes/entity.md) | (entity reference)             |
| plane                 | \[plane\](/docs/classes/plane.md)   | {normal = {0,0,1}, dist = 0.0} |
| startpos              | \[vector\](/docs/classes/vector.md) | {0.0, 0.0, 0.0}                |

# game\\\_event

\`\`\`lua
cheat.register\_callback("player\_death", function(event)
    local userid = event:get\_int("userid") -- get the userid of the victim
    event:set\_bool("headshot", true) -- show a fake headshot icon in the killfeed
    local distance = event:get\_float("distance") -- distance to the victim
end)
\`\`\`

{% hint style="info" %}
A list of game events and their structure information can be found \[here\](https://wiki.alliedmods.net/Counter-Strike:\_Global\_Offensive\_Events).
{% endhint %}

Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/cheat/register\_callback.md).

# register\\\_callback

\`\`\`lua
cheat.register\_callback(event\_id, func)

-- example using built-in event
cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function()
    print("Hello World") -- prints text every frame
end)

-- use game event instead of built-in event
cheat.register\_callback("weapon\_fire", function(event)
    local weapon\_name = event:get\_string("weapon")
    print(weapon\_name)
end)

-- example without in-line functions
local function run\_event(event)
    local item = event:get\_string("item")
    print("someone picked up " .. item)
end

cheat.register\_callback("item\_pickup", run\_event)
\`\`\`

Register an event callback. Used for running code when something happens in-game (bomb is planted, new round starts, player dies etc.)

{% hint style="info" %}
The currently available callback events are:

\* PreDraw
\* Draw
\* CreateMove
\* FrameStageNotify
\* Unload
\* VoiceData
\* Game Events (\[click here\](https://wiki.alliedmods.net/Counter-Strike:\_Global\_Offensive\_Events))
  {% endhint %}

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`event\_id\` (\`string\`): a callback event ID.
\* \`func\` (\`function\`): a function to execute on the execution of the specified event.


---

# rect\\\_filled

\`\`\`lua
render.rect\_filled(x, y, width, height, color, \[rounding\])
\`\`\`

Draws a filled rectangle.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`x\` (\`float\`): the x-coordinate of the top-left corner.
\* \`y\` (\`float\`): the y-coordinate of the top-left corner.
\* \`width\` (\`float\`): the width of the rectangle.
\* \`height\` (\`float\`): the height of the rectangle.
\* \`color\` (\[color\](/docs/libraries/color.md)): the fill color.
\* \`rounding\` (\`float\`, optional): rounds the corners of the rectangle. Defaults to \`0.0\`.


---

# send\\\_data

\`\`\`lua
utils.send\_data(bits)
\`\`\`

Sends raw data through a custom network buffer (used in exploits/hv packets/etc).

#### \*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`bits\` (\`uint64\_t\`): data to send.

#### Notes:&#x20;

\* Make sure the server supports or expects this, or it may result in a kick.


---

# vector2d

\`\`\`lua
local vec = vector2d(50, 100)
print(vec:x(), vec:y())
print("Length:", vec:length())

-- Default constructor
local a = vector2d()

-- With values
local b = vector2d(50, 100)
\`\`\`

| Member        | Type     | Example Value |
| ------------- | -------- | ------------- |
| x             | float    | 50.0          |
| y             | float    | 100.0         |
| length        | float    | 111.80        |
| length\\\_sqr   | float    | 12500.0       |
| is\\\_zero      | boolean  | false         |
| is\\\_valid     | boolean  | true          |
| zero          | function | \`vec:zero()\`  |
| dist\\\_to      | float    | 25.0          |
| dist\\\_to\\\_sqr | float    | 625.0         |

# find\\\_signature

\`\`\`lua
utils.find\_signature(module, signature)
\`\`\`

Finds a memory address using a signature scan.

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \`module\` (\`string\`):name of the module (\`client.dll\`, etc).
\* \`signature\` (\`string\`): IDA-style pattern (e.g. \`"55 8B ?? EC 83 EC"\`).

#### \*\*Returns:\*\*

\* \`uintptr\_t\`: pointer to the interface.


---

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/voice\_packet.md).

# voice\\\_packet

\`\`\`lua
cheat.register\_callback("VoiceData", function(packet)
    print("Voice data from entity: " .. tostring(packet:entity()))
    print("Data length: " .. #packet:bits())
end)

\`\`\`

| Member                       | Type       | Description                                                      |
| ---------------------------- | ---------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------- |
| \`bits\`                       | \`string\`   | Raw encoded voice data as a string (likely binary or compressed) |
| \`entity\`                     | \`entity\`   | Entity that belongs to the voice packet.                         |
| \`xuid\_low\`                   | \`uint32\_t\` | Lower 32 bits of the player's XUID                               |
| \`xuid\_high\`                  | \`uint32\_t\` | Upper 32 bits of the player's XUID                               |
| \`section\_number\`             | \`uint32\_t\` | Voice stream section number (useful for packet ordering)         |
| \`uncompressed\_sample\_offset\` | \`uint32\_t\` | Sample offset in the full uncompressed stream                    |
| \`sequence\_bytes\`             | \`uint32\_t\` | Packet sequence bytes                                            |
| \`format\`                     | \`int32\_t\`  | Audio encoding format ID (engine-specific)                       |


---

### CBaseAnimatingOverlay <a href="#cbaseanimatingoverlay" id="cbaseanimatingoverlay"></a>

\`\`\`
table DT\_BaseAnimatingOverlay
    parent DT\_BaseAnimating

# player | onetap Reloaded

For the complete documentation index, see [llms.txt](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt)
. This page is also available as [Markdown](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/classes/player.md)
.

Example usage:

Copy

    cheat.register_callback("player_death", function(event)
    
        local victim = entities.get_entity_from_user_id(event:get_int("userid"))
        local attacker = entities.get_entity_from_user_id(event:get_int("attacker"))
        
        if not attacker and not victim then
            return
        end
        
        if not attacker then
            if victim:IsLocalPlayer() then
                print("You just killed yourself! 🚑")
            end
        else
            if attacker:IsLocalPlayer() then
                print("You just killed " .. victim:GetName() .. "!")
            elseif victim:IsLocalPlayer() then
                print("Uh-oh! You were killed by " .. attacker:GetName() .. "!"
            end
        end
    
    end)

# Unknown

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/globals/frametime.md).

# frametime

\`\`\`lua
local delta = globals.frametime()

cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function()

    delta = globals.frametime()
    -- delta = 1.0 / globals.framerate() -- this achieves the same result
    print("Time since last frame: " .. delta .. "ms")

end)
\`\`\`

Returns the time that has passed since the last frame.\\
Calculated using the formula \`delta = 1.0 / FPS\`   \\
&#x20;            &#x20;

## Returns:

\`float\`: frame time.


---

# get\\\_teammates

\`\`\`lua
local teammates = entities.get\_teammates()
\`\`\`

Returns all teammates.

\*\*Returns:\*\*

\* List of \[player\](/docs/classes/player.md) objects currently on your team as a \`table\`.

\> For the complete documentation index, see \[llms.txt\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/llms.txt). Markdown versions of documentation pages are available by appending \`.md\` to page URLs; this page is available as \[Markdown\](https://onetap.gitbook.io/docs/libraries/ui/add\_checkbox.md).

# add\\\_checkbox

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_checkbox(name)
\`\`\`

Adds a checkbox to the menu.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`name\` (\`string\`): identifier/label for the checkbox.

#### Notes:

\* Value can be accessed with \[get\\\_bool\](/docs/libraries/ui/get\_bool.md).

\*\*\*

#### Example:

Print "I'm checked!" every frame the checkbox is checked.

\`\`\`lua
ui.add\_checkbox("Check me!")

cheat.register\_callback("Draw", function()
    if ui.get\_bool("Check me!") then
        print("I'm checked!")
    end
end)
\`\`\`

# execute\\\_command

\`\`\`lua
cheat.execute\_command(command)
\`\`\`

Execute a console command.

\*\*Parameters:\*\*

\* \`command\` (\`string\`): a console command

\*\*Notes:\*\*

\* The function will not run if the \`command\` parameter is empty.
